25:786:59673:33:18:72:540:174:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:In view of the many deconvolution operations, and the slow convergence rates of estimators
25:787:59763:18:18:72:540:156:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:based on deconvolution, this identification argument cannot be taken directly to data unless
25:788:59855:18:18:72:540:138:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the data set is very large indeed.  In our application, where we use a similar demand system,
25:789:59948:18:0:72:398:120:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:we impose a number of parametric assumptions to be practical.
26:790:60011:0:32:72:212:671:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:4.4    Reserve Prices
26:791:60032:32:18:72:540:639:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:In  many  markets,  sellers  set  reserve  prices  on  their  items.   They  do  this  to  avoid  selling
26:792:60137:18:18:72:540:621:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:them at a price below their best outside use (either retained by the seller, sold in a different
26:793:60233:18:18:72:540:603:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:market,  or  sold  in  this  market  at  a  later  date),  and  to  extract  more  money  from  buyers.
26:794:60336:18:18:72:540:585:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Sellers may set reserves non-strategically (e.g.  at cost, or the $1 starting bid recommended
26:795:60429:18:18:72:540:567:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:for many products on eBay), or to maximize expected revenue.  They will generally know
26:796:60515:18:18:72:540:549:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:everything commonly known by the bidders, which may include characteristics latent to the
26:797:60604:18:18:72:540:531:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:econometrician.10Reserves  are  sometimes  implemented  as  minimum  bids,  which  restrict
26:798:60695:18:18:71:539:513:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:participations to types with sufficiently high values (e.g.  on eBay).  In other settings (e.g.
26:799:60790:18:18:71:539:495:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:online advertising), the reserve may only be applied after the bids have been recorded (“secret
26:800:60885:18:24:71:346:477:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:reserves”), in order to adjust allocation and payment.
26:801:60939:24:18:71:539:453:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Reserve prices can be easily accounted for in the model.  Suppose that sellers charge reserve
26:802:61032:18:18:71:539:435:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:prices on each item sold, drawn iid from distributions{GRj}. We assume that buyers know the
26:803:61123:18:18:72:539:417:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:distributions of reserve prices.  Re-defineG1jas the conditional distribution of the maximum
26:804:61215:18:18:71:540:399:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of  the  highest  competing  bid  and  the  reserve  price  on  productj,  and  let  assumption  1
26:805:61313:18:18:72:540:381:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:hold as before.  Bids are equal to valuation less continuation value, where the continuation
26:806:61405:18:18:72:540:363:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:value is dependent on the distribution of reserve prices.  High reserve prices directly depress
26:807:61500:18:18:72:540:345:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:continuation values by lowering the likelihood that a bidder is successful in future auctions.
26:808:61594:18:24:72:455:327:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:They also mean fewer bidders exiting the market, toughening competition.
26:809:61666:24:18:72:540:303:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f9:B:For identification, the functionξ(·) still offers a valid inversion, though the distributions{G1j}
26:810:61764:18:15:72:540:285:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:are now amended to reflect the reserves.  So if we can identify the pseudo-type distribution
26:811:61856:15:27:72:507:270:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f3:B: ̃F, we can boundF.  With secret reserves, we can pointwise identify ̃Fjust as before.
26:812:61942:27:18:72:540:243:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:On the other hand, with minimum bids, we again face a selection problem:  only bids that
26:813:62030:18:18:72:540:225:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:clear  the  minimum  bid  will  be  observed.   So  in  the  selection  correction  step,  we  need  to
26:814:62133:18:18:72:540:207:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:take into account the reserves in calculatingsH(b).  Moreover — in contrast to all the prior
26:815:62225:18:18:72:540:189:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:analysis — some types might never be observed.11For example, suppose there is only one
26:816:62311:18:18:72:540:171:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:product, and it always gets a $100 reserve.  Then types with values below $100 will never
26:817:62400:18:18:72:540:153:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:bid.  The mass of such types cannot be inferred from the data.  This implies that we can only
26:818:62493:18:16:81:540:135:7:g_d0_f6:10:g_d0_f7:F:10For example, Roberts (2013) explores a model in which an unobserved heterogeneity termξis observed
26:819:62593:16:12:72:540:119:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:by sellers and used to set reserve prices.  He shows that the reserve prices can then be used as controls in
26:820:62701:12:8:72:158:107:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:estimating demand.
26:821:62719:8:16:81:539:99:7:g_d0_f6:10:g_d0_f7:F:11In the baseline model, every type bids on at least one product with positive probability.  This remains
26:822:62824:16:11:72:540:83:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:true in the limited data case,  since there is always some chance of being one of the top two bidders (e.g.
26:823:62931:11:0:72:274:72:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:when no other bidders are active that period).
27:824:62979:0:18:72:539:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:identify ̃Ffor the subset of types who bid on at least one product with positive probability.
27:825:63072:18:18:72:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:And  even  conditioning  on  types  that  bid  with  positive  probability,  we  can  only  partially
27:826:63173:18:18:72:540:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:identify ̃F.  This translates into weaker bounds onF, though the right tail of valuations will
27:827:63267:18:45:72:489:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:still be well-identified, and this is often what is needed for policy counterfactuals.
27:828:63353:45:32:72:224:572:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:4.5    Outside Options
27:829:63375:32:18:72:540:540:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We conclude our extensions with a variation of the model in which there are latent outside
27:830:63465:18:18:72:539:522:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f4:B:options. We introduce outside options by describing a more general environment withpassive
27:831:63555:18:18:72:540:504:12:g_d0_f4:12:g_d0_f3:B:search.  In each periodt, both new entrants and active incumbents are presented with either
27:832:63646:18:18:72:539:486:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:an auction of one of the goods inJ(as in the basic model), or an opportunity to buy one of
27:833:63736:18:18:72:539:468:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the goods inJat a fixed price in another market (observed by the bidder, unobserved to the
27:834:63826:18:18:72:540:450:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:econometrician).  Beliefs about opposing bids in the auction market follow Assumption 1,
27:835:63914:18:18:72:540:432:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and  are  captured  by  the  distributionsGAj(we  switch  superscript  to  indicate  “auction”).
27:836:64010:18:18:71:539:414:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Prices in the outside market are stochastic, sampled independently and identically over time
27:837:64102:18:18:71:539:396:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:according to product-specific continuous distributionsGOj(where the “O” stands for outside)
27:838:64193:18:18:72:540:378:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:with strictly positive density over their support.  We make a support inclusion assumption:
27:839:64284:18:18:72:539:360:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:supp(GOj)⊆supp(GAj), so that the highest bid in the auction market would always suffice
27:840:64371:18:18:72:540:342:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:to buy the corresponding good in the fixed price market.  This assumption seems weak given
27:841:64461:18:18:72:540:324:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:our intuitions about the size of price fluctuations in auction versus fixed price markets.  We
27:842:64555:18:24:72:272:306:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:make use of it in our arguments below.
27:843:64593:24:18:72:540:282:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Search in this environment is “passive” in the sense that active bidders do not actively choose
27:844:64688:18:18:72:540:264:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:which product to bid on,  nor whether to go to the fixed price or auction market.  This is
27:845:64778:18:18:72:540:246:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:consistent  with  our  initial  model.12But  bidders  are  sophisticated  and  take  into  account
27:846:64876:18:24:72:331:228:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:future opportunities when making decisions today.
27:847:64925:24:18:72:540:204:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:The transition matrix ̃Qis now of size 2J×2J, indicating the distribution over options that a
27:848:65018:18:18:72:539:186:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:bidder participating on some productjin one of the two markets{Auction,Fixed Price}will
27:849:65105:18:18:72:540:168:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:encounter when next active.  We simplify by assuming that this distribution is independent
27:850:65195:18:18:72:540:150:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of the past state, so that it is multinomial (πA,πO), where the J-vectorπAis the distribution
27:851:65288:18:9:72:539:132:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:over  theJproducts  offered  at  auction,πOis  the  distribution  over  outside  options,  and
27:852:65382:9:13:72:85:123:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:∑
27:853:65383:13:0:84:97:110:8:g_d0_f10:12:g_d0_f8:A:jπ
27:854:65385:0:7:98:104:118:8:g_d0_f10:8:g_d0_f10:A:A

27:857:65389:13:0:132:145:110:8:g_d0_f10:12:g_d0_f8:A:jπ

27:860:65468:15:16:72:540:96:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:inferences about the Markovian transitions between unobserved states in the outside market.

29:969:69829:18:0:72:539:91:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:probability of exit in the fixed price market isk(bj)  =k(bj)  =  (1−r) +r ̃πOjGOj(bj) and
30:970:69921:0:38:72:441:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:consequently their exit probability upon losing in the auction market is:
30:971:69994:38:0:197:291:633:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f8:A:e(bj) = (1−r) +r

30:974:70033:0:9:322:327:634:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:A:(

30:978:70106:39:0:214:261:557:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f8:C:e′(bj) =r

30:983:70132:22:0:263:293:548:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f8:?:(1−r
30:984:70136:0:10:296:301:558:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:(

30:988:70153:30:18:72:540:518:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f9:B:which  is  a  separable  first-order  ordinary  differential  equation  inGOj(b).   For  fixedr,{πj}
30:989:70253:18:18:72:539:500:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:ande′(bj),  this  equation  has  a  unique  solution  forGOj(b)  (see  appendix).   Then  sincer,
30:990:70350:18:19:72:539:482:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f3:B:{πj}ande′(bj) are identified, so isGOj(b) for eachj, which by earlier arguments suffices to
30:991:70441:19:18:72:540:463:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:identifyξ(·).  To use this function to bound the distribution of typesF, we need to identify
30:992:70533:18:18:72:539:445:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the distribution of pseudo-types ̃F, which requires a selection correction argument.  But the
30:993:70626:18:18:72:540:427:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:argument in Lemma 3 suffices for this, since the presence of an outside market doesn’t affect
30:994:70719:18:28:72:539:409:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the probability of the particular sequence of eventsHconsidered in that proof. Summarizing:
30:995:70810:28:18:72:540:381:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f4:F:Theorem 5(Identification with an outside option).Suppose Assumption 2 holds, and
30:996:70890:18:51:72:517:363:12:g_d0_f4:12:g_d0_f4:C:that supp(GOj)⊆supp(GAj)for everyj.  ThenFis partially identified, according to (6).
30:997:70974:51:35:71:286:312:17:g_d0_f2:17:g_d0_f2:C:5    Empirical Application
30:998:71000:35:18:71:539:277:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We  present  an  application  of  our  identification  result  to  the  auction  market  for  compact
30:999:71101:18:19:71:539:259:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:cameras on eBay.com.  We selected this market as an illustration for several reasons.  First,
30:1000:71194:19:18:71:539:240:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:as noted earlier, the eBay auction design is strategically similar to a sequence of second-price
30:1001:71290:18:18:71:539:222:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:sealed bid auctions.  Second, most consumers only purchase a single camera, so the unit de-
30:1002:71381:18:18:71:539:204:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:mand assumption seems reasonable.  Third, compact cameras are measurably differentiated
30:1003:71468:18:18:71:539:186:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:in a salient characteristic — namely resolution — which consumers may value differently,
30:1004:71556:18:18:71:539:168:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:affording us an opportunity to highlight a random coefficients variation of our model.  The
30:1005:71647:18:18:71:539:150:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:demand  model  we  estimate  allows  for  random  consumer  preferences  for  resolution  in  the
30:1006:71744:18:18:71:539:132:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:spirit  of  Berry  et  al.  (1995),  but  in  the  “pure  characteristics”  setting  of  Berry  and  Pakes
30:1007:71850:18:18:71:539:114:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:(2007).  We estimate the parameters of this model using a maximum likelihood approach
30:1008:71935:18:0:71:527:96:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and use those estimates to characterize consumer surplus and optimal bidding strategies.
31:1009:72025:0:32:72:303:671:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:5.1    Data and Market Overview
31:1010:72056:32:18:72:540:639:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:The  eBay  Marketplace.eBay  is  widely  considered  to  be  the  world  leader  in  online
31:1011:72147:18:18:72:540:621:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:auctions.  Various elements of its platform design, such as the use of proxy bidding agents,
31:1012:72239:18:18:72:540:603:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:feedback scores and “buy-it-now” offers have been widely copied.  At any time, eBay hosts a
31:1013:72330:18:18:72:540:585:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:large number of object listings from a variety of sellers.  Buyers can browse these, either by
31:1014:72424:18:18:72:540:567:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:navigating through categories delineated by the site, or by directly searching for key phrases.
31:1015:72519:18:18:72:540:549:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:For  example,  a  search  for  “digital  compact  camera”  will  typically  bring  up  thousands  of
31:1016:72619:18:18:72:540:531:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:listings.  Some of these are offered at “buy-it-now,” i.e.  fixed, prices.  As Einav et al. (2016)
31:1017:72717:18:18:72:540:513:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:have documented, over 60% of listings on eBay are now at fixed prices (though auctions were
31:1018:72808:18:18:72:540:495:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:more common at the time our data was collected).  We will ignore the presence of a fixed
31:1019:72896:18:18:72:540:477:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:price market in what follows, effectively ignoring substitution opportunities between the two
31:1020:72989:18:24:72:437:459:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:markets in favor of focusing on substitution within the auction market.
31:1021:73060:24:18:72:540:435:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Restricting  to  auctions  yields  a  list  of  items,  ordered  by  time  until  auction  end.   These
31:1022:73163:18:18:72:540:417:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:auctions all end at different times, so bidders face a set ofsequentialauctions. Unsurprisingly,
31:1023:73259:18:18:72:540:399:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:there is substantial heterogeneity in the cameras offered, in terms of brand, resolution, zoom
31:1024:73353:18:18:72:540:381:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and accessories (to name some of the most salient features).  Bidders can research past prices
31:1025:73447:18:24:72:350:363:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:for different items by searching the completed listings.
31:1026:73503:24:18:72:540:339:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Bids  are  placed  through  eBay’s  proprietary  “proxy  bidding”  system.   Bidders  enter  the
31:1027:73599:18:18:72:540:321:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:maximum they are willing to pay for the item, and then eBay’s proxy bidding system will
31:1028:73686:18:18:72:540:303:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:bid  up  from  the  current  standing  price  in  standardized  increments  on  their  behalf  until
31:1029:73786:18:18:72:540:285:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:either their bid is the highest yet entered in the system, or an additional increment would
31:1030:73877:18:18:72:540:267:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:take them over their maximum.  For example, if bidder A enters a bid of $8000 on a camera
31:1031:73966:18:18:72:540:249:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:where  the  standing  price  is  $6000  and  the  highest  bid  placed  in  the  system  by  a  rival  is
31:1032:74071:18:18:72:540:231:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:$7000, then the system will update the standing price to $7100 ($7000 + $100 increment),
31:1033:74159:18:18:72:540:213:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and will record this bidder as the currently high bidder.  Under unit demand high bidders
31:1034:74248:18:19:72:540:195:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:become  “committed”  to  the  auctions  they  enter,  in  the  sense  that  if  they  bid  in  another
31:1035:74350:19:23:72:415:176:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:auction, there is a risk of winning a second object they don’t need.
31:1036:74418:23:18:72:540:153:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Fear of premature commitment is perhaps one reason why bidders tend to bid late in auctions.
31:1037:74510:18:18:72:540:135:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:For example, on eBay Motors, 75% of bids are placed in the last day of the auction (Lewis,
31:1038:74600:18:18:72:540:117:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:2007).  Similar results have been found elsewhere on eBay and in other auction markets, and
31:1039:74691:18:18:72:540:99:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:a wide range of alternative explanations for late bidding have been offered (see e.g.  Roth and
31:1040:74786:18:0:72:540:81:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Ockenfels (2002)).  The combination of late and proxy bidding suggest that eBay’s auction
32:1041:74877:0:18:72:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:market is well approximated as a sequence of second-price sealed bid auctions, so that our
32:1042:74967:18:41:72:260:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:model can be applied to this setting.
32:1043:75004:41:18:72:540:612:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Data.We purchased a dataset concerning all sales of digital compact cameras over a 2-year
32:1044:75093:18:18:72:540:594:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:period from TeraPeak, a data analytics company The data includes attributes of the camera
32:1045:75182:18:18:72:540:576:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:auctioned (resolution, zoom, brand, product name, bundling of a tripod, extra battery etc),
32:1046:75273:18:18:72:540:558:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:attributes of the listing (starting price, secret reserve, listing title), and the outcome of the
32:1047:75370:18:18:72:540:540:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:auction. Each listing may be associated with several bids, all of which we observe — including
32:1048:75464:18:18:72:540:522:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the highest bid, which is not visible on the website and typically unavailable in “scraped”
32:1049:75555:18:18:72:540:504:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:auction datasets from the platform.  Market participants are persistent in our dataset — as
32:1050:75646:18:18:72:540:486:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:in our model — and we observe their attributes (feedback, location) and construct measures
32:1051:75736:18:24:72:331:468:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of experience and activity from observed behavior.
32:1052:75786:24:18:72:539:444:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We  work  with  a  subset  of  the  data,  consisting  only  ofnewcompact  cameras,  sold  in  the
32:1053:75884:18:18:72:540:426:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:3-month period between February 5th and May 6th of 2007.  We restrict attention to new
32:1054:75970:18:18:72:540:408:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:cameras to limit the influence of unobserved heterogeneity, though as we will see, this is still
32:1055:76066:18:18:72:540:390:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:a substantial problem.  We analyze this particular time period because supply was relatively
32:1056:76158:18:18:72:540:372:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:stable over those 3 months, so the stationarity assumptions implicit in our calculations of
32:1057:76249:18:18:72:540:354:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the continuation values are reasonable.  We pick cameras with the most common resolution
32:1058:76337:18:18:72:540:336:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:levels:  those with (rounded) resolution between 5 megapixels and 10 megapixels (MP). We
32:1059:76425:18:18:72:540:318:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:clean the data by excluding auctions with missing data, potential shill bidding, outlying bids
32:1060:76519:18:19:72:540:300:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and auctions that are terminated by the first bidder exercising a buy-it-now option (this is
32:1061:76611:19:23:72:459:281:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:unusual).  See the data appendix for further details on sample construction.
32:1062:76687:23:18:72:540:258:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:This  leaves  us  with  a  dataset  of  19160  auctions,  4387  sellers  and  74375  unique  bidders.
32:1063:76788:18:18:72:540:240:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Summary statistics are presented in Table 1.  In the top panel, we summarize the data at an
32:1064:76879:18:18:72:540:222:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:auction level (i.e.  an observation is an auction).  The average gap between the winning bid
32:1065:76971:18:18:72:540:204:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and the closing price is $10.60.  This is a direct estimate of the average consumer surplus
32:1066:77062:18:19:72:540:186:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of  winning  bidders  in  a  static  auction  model,  but  we  will  show  that  it  is  a  substantial
32:1067:77165:19:18:72:540:167:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:underestimate once continuation value is taken into account.  The probability of sale is quite
32:1068:77259:18:18:72:540:149:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:high, at 0.95.  Those products that do not sell tend to be among the small handful which
32:1069:77347:18:18:72:540:131:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:employ “secret reserve prices”, whereby the item only sells if the highest bid meets a reserve
32:1070:77441:18:18:72:540:113:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:price set by the seller but hidden from bidders.  On average an auction attracts 7 – 8 unique
32:1071:77534:18:23:72:394:95:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:bidders, and 16 – 17 bids, though there is substantial variance.
32:1072:77598:23:0:72:540:72:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Table 1 also summarizes the data at the seller and bidder level.  There are just over four
33:1073:77690:0:18:72:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:listings for every seller in our marketplace.  The distribution of seller shares is skewed, with
33:1074:77786:18:18:72:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:large, experienced sellers making up the bulk of listings.  However there are many such large
33:1075:77879:18:18:72:539:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:sellers and the seller concentration measure (HHI) remains low at 0.04.  On the bidders’ side
33:1076:77972:18:19:72:540:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:we find some motivation for the assumptions of our model Most bidders are unsuccessful in
33:1077:78061:19:18:72:540:598:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:acquiring an item (the purchase rate is 24.3%), but they are active in the market for nearly a
33:1078:78155:18:18:72:540:580:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:week and on average are observed bidding in two different auctions, with some participating
33:1079:78246:18:18:72:539:562:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:in many more than that.13This repeated participation is not driven by multi-unit demand—
33:1080:78334:18:45:72:409:544:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:99% of our bidders make one or fewer compact camera purchases.
33:1081:78396:45:31:72:254:499:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:5.2    Descriptive evidence
33:1082:78423:31:18:72:540:468:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Having introduced the data, we now offer some descriptive evidence that indicates our model
33:1083:78514:18:40:72:420:450:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:is a reasonable approximation to the behavior we see in the market.
33:1084:78581:40:19:72:539:410:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Do bidders substitute across products?If bidders generally bid on the same products
33:1085:78664:19:18:72:540:391:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:repeatedly (or have identical preferences over product characteristics), one might think that
33:1086:78757:18:18:72:540:373:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the single-good models familiar from the existing empirical auctions literature may suffice.
33:1087:78849:18:18:72:540:355:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:So to get some evidence on this, we look for evidence of substitution across products.  There
33:1088:78942:18:18:72:540:337:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:are many distinct products sold in our dataset, but in the demand system below we allow
33:1089:79029:18:18:72:540:319:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:random coefficients over camera resolution, and so this is the relevant definition of a product
33:1090:79124:18:18:72:540:301:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:for the purposes of our analysis.  We therefore calculate a transition matrix across cameras of
33:1091:79219:18:18:72:540:283:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:different resolution, shown in Table 2.  Each entry in the matrix is the probability (expressed
33:1092:79314:18:18:72:540:265:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:as a percentage) that a bidder who bids on a camera of the resolution in a given row subse-
33:1093:79405:18:18:72:540:247:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:quently bids on a camera with the column resolution.  We find that most buyers that bid on
33:1094:79495:18:18:72:540:229:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:multiple cameras tend to bid on a product with the same resolution next, but the probability
33:1095:79587:18:18:72:540:211:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of this is far away from 100%, ranging from 45.5% to 80.5%.  When they substitute, they
33:1096:79674:18:18:72:540:193:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:tend to pick a product of similar resolution (the biggest off-diagonal elements are generally
33:1097:79767:18:41:72:185:175:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:close to the diagonal).
33:1098:79790:41:18:72:540:134:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Do bidders have option value?Another focus of our approach has been to emphasize
33:1099:79870:18:18:72:540:116:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:dynamic bidding and option values.  Option values arise from price fluctuations — a bid that
33:1100:79962:18:18:72:540:98:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:loses today may win tomorrow.  Many economists have the intuition that in large markets
33:1101:80049:18:0:81:539:80:7:g_d0_f6:10:g_d0_f7:F:13We say a bidder is “active” from the start of the first auction they bid in to the end of the last auction.

34:1134:81117:27:12:72:540:183:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:Notes:  Summary statistics for the full dataset, which consists of all auctions of compact cameras auctions
34:1135:81224:12:12:72:540:171:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:on a large online platform that ended during the period Feb 5 – May 6, 2007.  Observations with missing
34:1136:81327:12:12:72:540:159:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:product characteristics have been dropped.  The “incumbent period” for a buyer is measured as the time
34:1137:81429:12:12:72:540:147:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:from the start-date of the first auction bid in to the end of the last auction bid in.  “Time between bids” is
34:1138:81539:12:12:72:540:135:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:the gap between the first and second bids by a buyer on different objects, measured only for the subsample
34:1139:81645:12:12:72:540:123:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:of bidders with multiple bids.  “Seller HHI” is the Herfidahl–Hirschman index for sellers, based on their share
34:1140:81756:12:0:72:513:111:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:of items sold.  “Buyer HHI” is the analogous measure for buyers, based on the share of items bought.

35:1148:82041:27:12:72:540:551:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:Notes:  Each entry in the matrix gives the observed frequency with which a bidder who is observed bidding
35:1149:82146:12:45:72:372:539:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:on the row product is next observed bidding on the column product.
35:1150:82212:45:18:72:540:494:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the law of one price holds,  and so price fluctuations should be minimal.  This is not true
35:1151:82303:18:18:72:540:476:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:here.  The top left panel of Figure 2 shows the median daily transaction prices (including
35:1152:82393:18:18:72:540:458:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:shipping)  on  different  models  of  camera,  over  the  sample  period.   There  is  quite  a  lot  of
35:1153:82497:18:18:72:540:440:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:variability — an typical change is 10% — and since it is a median price, this is not driven
35:1154:82588:18:24:72:172:422:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:entirely by outliers.
35:1155:82609:24:18:72:540:398:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:To rule out variation based on compositional effects, we drilled down to look at the highest
35:1156:82701:18:18:72:540:380:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:volume seller’s most popular product (a Kodak Easyshare Z710), and plotted the price series
35:1157:82792:18:18:72:540:362:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:against time (fluctuations could be within a day), shown in the top right panel of Figure 2.
35:1158:82884:18:18:72:540:344:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Prices vary from below $200 to over $250 dollars.  Doing some rough back of the envelope
35:1159:82972:18:18:72:540:326:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:calculations based on the observed price distribution, a bidder with a valuation of $250 (red
35:1160:83065:18:18:72:540:308:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:dashed line), bidding once a day, with a daily exit hazard rate of 0.5, should optimally shade
35:1161:83159:18:18:72:540:290:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:their bid down to $238 (green dashed line), because of the option value (and should expect
35:1162:83249:18:19:72:540:272:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:to  pay  closer  to  $225,  yellow  dashed  line).   Indeed  this  option  value  should  be  present  in
35:1163:83354:19:18:72:540:253:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:many online markets:  Einav et al. (2011) have found the standard deviation in price to be
35:1164:83444:18:23:72:426:235:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:on the order of 10% of the transaction price in most eBay categories.
35:1165:83513:23:18:72:540:212:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We also observe that the average time between bids is just over four days, with many auctions
35:1166:83606:18:18:72:540:194:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:closing in the meantime.  This suggests that bidders are inattentive (i.e.τclose to zero).  In
35:1167:83700:18:19:72:540:176:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:view of this, Assumption 1 seems quite reasonable:  information from the current auction is
35:1168:83791:19:40:72:520:157:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:probably a poor predictor of what conditions will be like the next time the bidder bids.
35:1169:83879:40:18:72:539:117:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Is  there  unobserved  product  heterogeneity?The  way  we  specify  valuations  below
35:1170:83965:18:18:72:540:99:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:incorporates random coefficients over camera resolution, as well as common preferences for
35:1171:84055:18:0:72:540:81:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:observable camera attributes (e.g.  brand) and an unobservable component.  To motivate the
36:1172:84188:0:7:91:293:562:3:Helvetica:3:Helvetica:?:Feb 01Mar 01Apr 01May 01

36:1180:84376:44:12:72:539:482:12:g_d0_f3:10:g_d0_f7:B:Figure 2:  Market Dynamics.The left panel shows the median daily price (including shipping) over the
36:1181:84476:12:12:72:540:470:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:sample period, separately by camera resolution (4MP cameras omitted for clarity).  The right panel shows
36:1182:84580:12:12:72:540:458:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:the closing transaction prices on auctions of a Kodak Easyshare Z710 from a single seller over the sample
36:1183:84685:12:12:72:540:446:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:period,  superimposing  over  this  the  valuation,  optimal  bid  and  expected  payment  of  a  bidder  with  $250
36:1184:84801:12:35:72:231:434:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:valuation (see text for more details).
36:1185:84839:35:18:72:540:399:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:inclusion of this unobserved product heterogeneity, we perform a simple heuristic estimation
36:1186:84931:18:18:72:540:381:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:exercise.  We take bids that have been “normalized” to account for observable heterogeneity
36:1187:85022:18:18:72:540:363:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:(we explain this process below), and look at bidders who have bid exactly twice on cameras
36:1188:85112:18:18:72:540:345:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:at two different resolution levels (e.g.  7MP and 8MP cameras).  Dividing the difference in
36:1189:85203:18:18:72:540:327:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:their normalized bids by the difference in the camera resolutions gives us a crude estimate
36:1190:85294:18:18:72:540:309:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of this bidder’s willingness to pay for megapixels, and the distribution of differences across
36:1191:85388:18:24:72:457:291:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:such bidders gives us an idea of the diversity in bidders’ willingness to pay.
36:1192:85466:24:18:72:540:267:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Figure 3 presents the density of that statistic computed at the bidder level for this restricted
36:1193:85562:18:18:72:540:249:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:subset,  without  any  kind  of  selection  correction.   While  the  mean  of  this  distribution  is
36:1194:85664:18:18:72:540:231:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:positive (reassuringly) and the variance is large (motivating heterogeneous preferences for
36:1195:85755:18:18:72:540:213:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:resolution), there is a troublesome and substantial mass to the left of zero.  It is implausible
36:1196:85851:18:18:72:540:195:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:that  many  consumers  have  negative  marginal  utility  from  higher  resolution  cameras,  and
36:1197:85948:18:18:72:540:177:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:we instead interpret this as evidence of unobserved product heterogeneity in our data that
36:1198:86038:18:0:72:454:159:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:confounds this simple approach (we will offer more direct evidence below).
37:1199:86114:0:0:72:181:422:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Figure 3:   Density of

37:1202:86230:11:35:71:539:407:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:difference in bids across cameras of two resolution levels and the difference in resolution levels, across bidders.
37:1203:86345:35:32:71:185:372:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:5.3    Estimation
37:1204:86362:32:18:71:539:340:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We  construct  a  demand  system  in  which  consumers  obtain  value  from  the  purchase  of  a
37:1205:86459:18:18:71:539:322:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:single  camera,  a  value  which  has  an  idiosyncratic  component  and  a  common  component.
37:1206:86554:18:33:71:457:304:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Formally, bidderi’s valuation for productjoffered in auctiontis given by:
37:1207:86627:33:8:220:324:271:12:g_d0_f8:8:g_d0_f10:?:xi,j,t=αi,c+ resjαi,r
37:1208:86648:8:10:257:324:263:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:︸︷︷︸
37:1209:86652:10:0:268:315:253:8:g_d0_f5:8:g_d0_f5:A:idiosyncratic
37:1210:86665:0:8:327:390:271:12:g_d0_f3:8:g_d0_f10:?:+Zj,tγ+ξj,t
37:1211:86676:8:10:338:390:263:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:︸︷︷︸
37:1212:86680:10:0:349:380:253:8:g_d0_f5:8:g_d0_f5:?:common
37:1213:86686:0:45:519:540:271:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:(14)
37:1214:86690:45:18:71:539:226:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:This  combines  the  random  coefficients  of  section  4.2,  and  the  unobserved  heterogeneity
37:1215:86787:18:18:71:540:208:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of  4.3.2  and  adds  some  observable  common  demand  shiftersZj,t.   Bidderi’s  type  in  our
37:1216:86883:18:18:71:540:190:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:model,αi, is a double:  their fixed utility draw for obtaining any camera (αic) as well as an
37:1217:86976:18:18:71:540:172:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:idiosyncratic preference shock for resolution (αir).  The auction-specific termξj,tcaptures
37:1218:87067:18:18:71:539:154:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:unobserved heterogeneity that is observable to all bidders but not the econometrician.  We
37:1219:87157:18:19:71:540:136:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:assume that it is distributed normally with mean zero and varianceσξ,jthat varies freely with
37:1220:87250:19:18:71:539:117:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the resolution type of the camera.  The bidder typeαiis drawn, iid upon bidder entry, from
37:1221:87340:18:18:71:539:99:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the distributionFα, which is our main estimation target.  We assume mutual independence
37:1222:87427:18:0:71:540:81:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of (αi,Zj,t,ξj).  On the supply side, we assume that the distribution of arriving auctions is
38:1223:87522:0:41:72:482:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:iid multinomial over the product space with aJ-vector of probability weightsπ.
38:1224:87600:41:18:72:539:630:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Estimation of supply and exit rates.Estimation begins with the recovery of the sur-
38:1225:87683:18:18:72:540:612:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:vival rater, and the multinomial supplyπ.  Note that with multinomial supply, the activity
38:1226:87773:18:18:72:539:594:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:rateτplays no role in optimal bidding and need not be estimated (whereas with Markov
38:1227:87857:18:18:72:540:576:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:supply transitionsQ,  the activity rate drives a wedge between supply transitions and the
38:1228:87946:18:37:72:175:558:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:state transitions ̃Q).
38:1229:87968:37:18:101:540:521:12:g_d0_f4:12:g_d0_f3:A:Survival  Rate  of  Bidders(r):  We estimate this parameter using a censored negative
38:1230:88053:18:18:101:540:503:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:binomial  model  fit  to  the  likelihood  of  bidder  exit  using  the  full  sample  of  bids.   A
38:1231:88153:18:18:101:540:485:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:bidder  exits  if  they  do  not  return  to  bid  again.   However  we  treat  this  outcome  as
38:1232:88250:18:28:101:468:467:12:g_d0_f3:8:g_d0_f5:A:censored if the last bid event was in the final six weeks of our dataset.14
38:1233:88325:28:40:101:501:439:12:g_d0_f4:12:g_d0_f3:A:Supply(π):  ˆπis the observed market share of each of the six resolution types.
38:1234:88404:40:18:72:540:399:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Bid normalization.Cameras differ in both observable and unobservable features.  The
38:1235:88487:18:18:72:540:381:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:first step in working with the bids is to normalize out the contribution of observables for
38:1236:88578:18:18:72:540:363:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:which bidders have common preferences (Haile et al., 2006).  Applying our earlier theory to
38:1237:88669:18:34:72:377:345:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the valuations in (14), the bidding equation takes the form:
38:1238:88729:34:33:164:540:311:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:A:bi,j,t= max{0,αi,c+ resjαi,r+Zj,tγ+ξj,t−v(αi,c,αi,r)}(15)
38:1239:88786:33:18:72:540:278:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:i.e.  valuation less continuation value.  Restricting attention to positive bids, and adding and
38:1240:88882:18:18:72:539:260:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:subtractingψj≡EFα[αi,c+ resjαi,r−v(αi,c,αi,r)], we get an estimating equation in reduced
38:1241:88970:18:18:72:99:242:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:form:
38:1242:88975:18:26:245:365:224:12:g_d0_f8:8:g_d0_f10:A:bi,j,t=ψj+Zj,tγ+ei,j,t
38:1243:88997:26:18:72:539:198:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:where the error termei,j,tcombines an individual-specific deviation in bid from that of the
38:1244:89088:18:18:72:540:180:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:average type and the common unobserved heterogeneity.  Since these are both independent
38:1245:89175:18:19:72:451:162:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:ofZj,t), we can estimateγconsistently by OLS with product fixed effects.
38:1246:89247:19:15:81:539:143:7:g_d0_f6:10:g_d0_f7:F:14We maintain the assumption of exogenous exit on the part of bidders, though it could be weakened using
38:1247:89351:15:12:72:540:128:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:the methods of Section 4.5.  While the assumption might seem somewhat unrealistic, we found no evidence
38:1248:89454:12:12:72:540:116:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:in reduced–form regressions of a systematic correlation between exit of losing bidders and the level of their
38:1249:89563:12:12:72:540:104:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:bid.  In the end, we chose to highlight the extensions that were most necessary to fit the basic features of
38:1250:89671:12:0:72:183:92:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:the data discussed above.
39:1251:89698:0:18:72:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We only run this regression on a subsample of our data, consisting of the two highest bids
39:1252:89788:18:18:72:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:in every auction.  This is motivated by the behavioral intuition of Haile and Tamer (2003).
39:1253:89879:18:18:72:540:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Because eBay’s proxy bidding system is formally an ascending auction, the bid of the third,
39:1254:89970:18:19:72:539:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:fourth,  orn-th  highest  bidder  may  not  reflect  their  intended  final  bid  (what  they  would
39:1255:90070:19:18:72:540:598:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:have bid in a sealed-bid auction i.e.  valuation less continuation value).  It is common for
39:1256:90162:18:18:72:540:580:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:bidders to “test out” a sequence of ascending bids to see if they can become the standing
39:1257:90251:18:18:72:540:562:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:high bidder, but if in this process the price comes to exceed their intended final bid then it
39:1258:90345:18:18:72:540:544:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:will be censored from the dataset.  For this reason we restrict attention to the two highest
39:1259:90437:18:24:72:363:526:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:bids in each auction, who are never censored in this way.
39:1260:90494:24:18:72:540:502:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:As  controlsZj,twe  include  product  line fixed  effects,  listing attributes  including  shipping
39:1261:90593:18:18:71:539:484:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:options,  seller feedback,  and  optional  listing features (e.g.,  sellers may  pay a fee for their
39:1262:90693:18:18:71:539:466:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:results to be highlighted in search results), as well as a set of dummies for resolution, optical
39:1263:90790:18:18:71:540:448:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:zoom, and digital zoom levels.15We report results for the main controls of interest in Table
39:1264:90882:18:18:71:539:430:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:3.  They are generally sensible, with bids increasing in seller feedback, decreasing in shipping
39:1265:90978:18:18:71:539:412:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:costs,  and particularly high for listings with free shipping,  consistent with the findings of
39:1266:91073:18:24:71:170:394:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Einav et al. (2011).
39:1267:91093:24:18:71:539:370:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Define the normalized bids ̃bi,j,t=bi,j,t−Zj,tγ=αi,c+resjαi,r−v(αi,c,αi,r)+ξj,t. We will work
39:1268:91186:18:18:72:540:352:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:with our estimate of these bidsbi,j,t−Zj,tˆγin what follows.  Consider the difference between
39:1269:91279:18:18:72:540:334:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:two  normalized  bids  on  the  same  product,  by  the  same  bidder  in  two  different  auctions.
39:1270:91379:18:18:72:539:316:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:These should differ only byξj,t1−ξj,t2, and since these random variables are independent of
39:1271:91470:18:18:72:539:298:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:each other, we can estimate the variance ofξj,tasσ2ξ,j=V ar(bi,j,t−bi,j,t′)/2 where the RHS
39:1272:91561:18:40:72:389:280:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:variance is estimated by pooling over allt < t′pairs available.
39:1273:91624:40:18:72:539:240:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Opposing bids.Recall from the identification analysis of section 4.3.2 that the relevant
39:1274:91712:18:18:72:540:222:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:strategic  object  for  bidders  to  form  beliefs  about  is{ˇG1j},  the  distribution  of  the  highest
39:1275:91817:18:18:72:540:204:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:competing bid net of unobserved heterogeneity (sinceξj,tjust acts as a common bid shifter).
39:1276:91908:18:19:72:540:186:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:So we need to estimate{ˇG1j}.  Also, for the reasons outlined above, we only want to use the
39:1277:92000:19:18:72:540:167:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:top two bids in each auction in estimation.  This places us in the “limited data” case, and
39:1278:92091:18:23:72:539:149:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:will require correcting for selection into the top two bids.  So we also need to estimate{ˇG2j}.
39:1279:92187:23:18:71:540:126:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f9:B:We observe the raw distributions of the first and second highest normalized bids{G1j,G2j}
39:1280:92276:18:19:71:539:108:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:(i.e.   the  convolution  ofˇbi,jandξj,t).   Based  on  the  shape  of  these,  we  assume  a  Gamma

42:1380:96581:23:18:71:539:277:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:This  computation  yields  a  substantially  larger  estimate  of  consumer  surplus  per  bidder:
42:1381:96679:18:18:71:539:259:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:((0.4354)−1×$2.73 = ) $6.04, or $24.35 per auction.  This large correction reflects the fact
42:1382:96771:18:19:71:539:241:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:that the bidders who are most likely to win also shade the most, and therefore it is for these
42:1383:96865:19:40:71:348:222:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:that the static model most underestimates valuations.
42:1384:96918:40:18:71:539:182:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Estimation of Demand.At this stage, we have estimates ofπ,rand the distributions
42:1385:96998:18:18:71:540:164:12:g_d0_f9:12:g_d0_f3:B:{G1j,G2j}of  first  and  second  order  statistics,  after  adjusting  for  observed  and  unobserved
42:1386:97099:18:18:71:539:146:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:heterogeneity.  We also have a dataset of normalized bids that were themselves first or second
42:1387:97193:18:18:71:539:128:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:highest bids in auctions, and therefore plausibly equal to valuation less continuation value.
42:1388:97286:18:15:81:540:110:7:g_d0_f6:10:g_d0_f7:F:17This relies on an assumption thatτis sufficiently small that each time a bidder participates, sufficient
42:1389:97392:15:12:71:540:95:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:time has passed that the market is once again in steady-state i.e.v(b) can be calculated without sophisticated
42:1390:97502:12:12:71:539:83:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:conditioning on histories.  We could be more mathematically precise — as we were in the earlier selection
42:1391:97607:12:0:71:462:71:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:correction argument — but as we argued when discussing Table 1,τappears to be small.
43:1392:97693:0:18:72:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:In principle, we could continue by applying our nonparametric identification strategy from
43:1393:97783:18:18:72:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Theorem 4 directly in estimation, for bidders who are observed bidding on each least two
43:1394:97871:18:18:72:540:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:different products (since the random coefficient is two-dimensional, two different products
43:1395:97962:18:19:72:540:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:suffices for identification).  But there are less than 300 such bidders in our dataset, and this
43:1396:98058:19:18:72:540:598:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:makes  the  necessary  deconvolution  analysis  unattractive  in  view  of  the  slow  convergence
43:1397:98156:18:23:72:350:580:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:properties of such estimators (Carroll and Hall, 2004).
43:1398:98211:23:18:72:540:557:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:So instead we take a parametric approach, assuming thatαcandαrare distributed Γ(kc,θc)
43:1399:98297:18:18:72:540:539:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and Γ(kr,θr), respectively.  We chose the gamma distribution because our estimation sample
43:1400:98387:18:19:72:540:521:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:consists of the right tail of bids, i.e.  first– and second– highest bids, and so we want a para-
43:1401:98484:19:18:72:539:502:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:metric model with flexibility to fit the shape of that tail.  Thereforeθ≡{kc,θc,kr,θr}makes
43:1402:98575:18:18:72:540:484:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:up the set of parameters of the demand system we ultimately hope to recover.  Following
43:1403:98662:18:18:72:540:466:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the logic of our non-parametric identification argument, we need to see bidders bid multiple
43:1404:98754:18:18:72:540:448:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:times in order to identify demand.  So we estimate the model using a sample of bidders who
43:1405:98844:18:18:72:540:430:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:submit either the first or second–highest bid in auctions on exactly two distinct resolution
43:1406:98936:18:18:72:540:412:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:types, a sample of 264 bidders (very few bidders come first or second on three or more dis-
43:1407:99027:18:18:72:540:394:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:tinct products, so we simplify the analysis by excluding their data).  Under our parametric
43:1408:99118:18:61:72:410:376:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:assumptions, we have the following likelihood of each observation:

44:1449:100244:41:18:72:540:630:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Estimating bid functions and selection probabilities.In order to compute the like-

44:1467:101544:18:18:71:539:299:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:outside of the setA ⊆ J.  DefineP(A,b,j) in the same way, but additionally conditioning

45:1489:102570:17:12:72:540:312:12:g_d0_f3:10:g_d0_f7:B:Figure 4:  Estimated Bid Functions and Selection Probabilities.This figure presents bid functions
45:1490:102667:12:35:72:451:300:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:and selection probabilities as a function ofαc, holding fixedαrat two levels:  0 and 20.
45:1491:102755:35:18:71:539:265:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:is for the case wherej6∈ A, and then the bidder mustnotbe observed inj, so they must
45:1492:102839:18:18:71:539:247:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:make a bid below the second highest.  Given that this is the case, again they must either
45:1493:102928:18:24:71:356:229:12:g_d0_f3:8:g_d0_f5:B:exit immediately or survive and we getP(A,b) again.19
45:1494:102981:24:18:71:540:205:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:NowG1jandG2jare known, andP(A,b) is a weighted sum of theP(A,b,j), so for any (A,b)
45:1495:103064:18:18:71:539:187:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:we can getP(A,b) as the solution to a linear system with unknowns{P(A,b,j)}j∈J.  Then
45:1496:103149:18:18:71:539:169:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:we can use these objects to compute the probability that a bidder is observed inexactlythe
45:1497:103239:18:18:71:539:151:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:setB.  For instance, if we are interested in the probability that a bidder of typeαis observed
45:1498:103333:18:18:71:539:133:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f9:B:in a subsetB={2,4}we can computeP({2,4}|β(α)}=P({2,4},β(α))−P({2},β(α))−
45:1499:103405:18:19:71:215:115:12:g_d0_f12:12:g_d0_f3:B:P({4},β(α)) +P({φ}|β(α)).
45:1500:103430:19:15:81:539:96:7:g_d0_f6:10:g_d0_f7:F:19This calculation assumes that the true state space coincides with the one that bidders use in forming
45:1501:103533:15:0:72:530:81:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:beliefs.  This is not necessary (we could condition on history), but is practical given our data constraints.
46:1502:103644:0:18:72:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Figure 4 illustrates the resulting bid functions and selection probabilities when these proce-
46:1503:103738:18:18:72:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:dures are applied to our data.  The selection probability is for the event that a bidder bids
46:1504:103831:18:18:72:539:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:on exactly two different products (|B|= 2), i.e.  that a bidder is selected into our estimation
46:1505:103926:18:19:72:539:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:sample.  Panel (a) shows the bid function for a bidder withαr= 0, i.e.  a bidder who places
46:1506:104017:19:18:72:540:598:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:no value on resolution, and consequently bids the same on every product.  Their bid function
46:1507:104109:18:18:72:540:580:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:“peels  away”  from  the  45-degree  line.   This  makes  intuitive  sense:  asαcincreases,  their
46:1508:104207:18:18:72:540:562:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:continuation value increases as well, causing them to shade their bids.  Panel (b) repeats this
46:1509:104302:18:18:72:539:544:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:exercise for the case whereαr= 20.  They now bid differently on each product, with the five
46:1510:104393:18:18:72:540:526:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:dotted lines showing their bids on the lowest resolution camera (bottom line) up to the top
46:1511:104484:18:18:72:539:508:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:resolution camera (top line), asαcvaries.  The shape is largely preserved, except that now
46:1512:104574:18:24:72:467:490:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:there is a positive intercept because valuations are positive even withαc= 0.
46:1513:104651:24:18:72:539:466:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:In panels (c) and (d) we show the selection probabilities for these two types of bidders (αr= 0
46:1514:104746:18:18:72:539:448:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:in (c) andαr= 20 in (d)) asαcvaries.  The “hump-shape” arises because the probability
46:1515:104831:18:18:72:539:430:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of|B|= 2 is increasing at first as the likelihood that the bidder is ever first or second rises,
46:1516:104927:18:18:72:540:412:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:but later declines as the probability that they win their first auction and exit before bidding
46:1517:105022:18:40:72:164:394:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:again goes to one.
46:1518:105040:40:18:72:539:354:12:g_d0_f2:12:g_d0_f3:B:Optimization.We now proceed to the problem of optimizing the likelihood.  Usually one
46:1519:105125:18:18:72:540:336:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:would proceed by applying some optimization routine in an outer loop to the likelihood (16),
46:1520:105217:18:18:72:539:318:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:evaluating it by Monte Carlo integration, holding the randomness in the draws ofαfixed
46:1521:105303:18:19:72:540:300:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:across evaluationsk(Pakes and Pollard, 1989).  But this is computationally costly,  as for
46:1522:105393:19:23:72:504:281:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:many differentαdraws we will have to evaluate the bidding and selection functions.
46:1523:105475:23:18:72:540:258:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Notice that the parameter vectorθenters the likelihood (16) only through the distribution
46:1524:105564:18:18:72:540:240:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of random coefficientsF(α|θ).  This allows us to employ an alternative approach based on
46:1525:105652:18:40:72:223:222:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:re-weighting.  Fixingα, define
46:1526:105682:40:0:193:232:182:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f9:?:hi(α)≡
46:1527:105688:0:17:237:292:191:12:g_d0_f12:12:g_d0_f9:?:P{Bi|b(α)}
46:1528:105698:17:0:239:290:174:12:g_d0_f12:12:g_d0_f9:?:P{φ|b(α)}
46:1529:105707:0:9:296:305:203:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:(
46:1530:105708:9:26:307:322:194:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:∏
46:1531:105709:26:0:305:323:168:8:g_d0_f10:6:g_d0_f14:?:j∈Bi
46:1532:105713:0:0:325:332:182:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f8:A:φ
46:1533:105714:0:8:334:343:199:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:(
46:1534:105715:8:17:344:394:191:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:?:bi−bj(α)
46:1535:105723:17:0:360:377:174:12:g_d0_f8:8:g_d0_f10:?:σξ,j
46:1536:105727:0:17:394:412:199:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:))
46:1537:105729:17:41:415:540:182:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:A:,(18)
46:1538:105734:41:18:72:540:141:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:and note that this object is computable for anyαfrom the results of the first-stage estimation.
46:1539:105829:18:34:72:530:123:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Therefore, taking as our objective function the log-likelihood of the dataset, we can write
46:1540:105920:34:0:213:274:89:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:?:L(θ,{bi}) =
46:1541:105931:0:25:277:294:100:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:∑

46:1545:105937:16:0:327:540:89:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:A:hi(α)dF(α|θ).(19)
47:1546:105956:0:18:72:539:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:One natural and computationally efficient way to proceed would then be to sampleαuni-
47:1547:106041:18:18:71:539:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:formly from the type spaceStimes (forSthe number of draws in the Monte Carlo inte-
47:1548:106123:18:18:71:539:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:gration), and then optimize the simulated criterion function by re-weighting their likelihood
47:1549:106216:18:19:71:540:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:contribution according tof(α|θ).  Instead, we choose to use importance sampling, i.e.  sam-
47:1550:106307:19:18:71:539:598:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:pling from and re-weighting relative to a user-chosen distribution, denotedG(α).  We do this
47:1551:106399:18:18:71:539:580:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:for two reasons: first, for efficiency — we would like to sample more points from the center of
47:1552:106494:18:18:71:539:562:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the true distribution if possible, since this is where the gradient of the likelihood is sharpest.
47:1553:106592:18:18:71:539:544:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Second, we would like the sampled distribution to have unbounded support, mirroring our
47:1554:106679:18:24:71:247:526:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:parametric assumption onF(α|θ).
47:1555:106710:24:37:71:362:502:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Let the set of points be drawn fromG(α); then we have:
47:1556:106764:37:13:178:239:465:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:ˆθ= arg max
47:1557:106775:13:0:217:221:452:8:g_d0_f10:8:g_d0_f10:?:θ
47:1558:106776:0:0:244:305:462:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:?:L(θ,{bi}) =
47:1559:106787:0:25:309:326:473:12:g_d0_f16:12:g_d0_f16:C:∑
47:1560:106788:25:0:316:319:448:8:g_d0_f10:8:g_d0_f10:A:i
47:1561:106789:0:0:328:343:462:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:?:log
47:1562:106792:0:29:351:362:477:8:g_d0_f10:12:g_d0_f16:?:S∑
47:1563:106794:29:0:346:361:448:8:g_d0_f10:8:g_d0_f5:?:s=1
47:1564:106797:0:0:364:391:462:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:?:hi(α)
47:1565:106802:0:16:392:430:470:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:?:f(αs|θ)
47:1566:106809:16:0:397:425:454:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:?:g(αs)
47:1567:106814:0:45:430:540:462:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:A:.(20)
47:1568:106819:45:18:71:540:417:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We implemented the estimator in two steps:  first, we chooseG1to be a normal with very
47:1569:106905:18:18:71:540:399:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:large variance, and obtained a first estimate ̃θ.  In a second step, we drew from a distribution
47:1570:107001:18:18:71:540:381:12:g_d0_f8:12:g_d0_f3:B:G2(α) =F(α| ̃θ) and re-optimized.  This two-step procedure should improve the efficiency
47:1571:107089:18:18:71:539:363:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of our estimator, as the second sample should be more centered and thus provide a better
47:1572:107177:18:45:71:225:345:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:approximation to the integral.
47:1573:107207:45:31:71:160:300:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:5.4    Results
47:1574:107221:31:19:71:539:269:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Estimates from this ML exercise are presented in Table 5.  Our results suggest that camera
47:1575:107311:19:18:71:539:250:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:resolution is the main determinant of consumer utility, but that there is substantial hetero-
47:1576:107404:18:18:71:539:232:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:geneity in how consumers value this attribute.  They predict a mean taste for cameras of
47:1577:107492:18:18:71:539:214:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:22.26  with  a  standard  deviation  of  51.06,  and  a  mean  taste  for  resolution  of  22.75  and  a
47:1578:107596:18:18:71:540:196:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:standard deviation of 6.41.  Recall that we have estimatedF, whereas the observed bids in
47:1579:107685:18:18:71:539:178:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the data (i.e., first- or second-highest bids) will tend to come from bidders sampled the right
47:1580:107780:18:24:71:188:160:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:tail of the distribution.
47:1581:107805:24:18:71:539:136:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:As a measure of goodness of fit we also compute moments of the bid distribution that were
47:1582:107894:18:18:71:539:118:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:not  used  directly  in  estimation.   In  Table  6  we  present  means  and  standard  errors  of  the
47:1583:107997:18:18:71:539:100:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:observed  bids  by  product  type  as  well  as  means  and  standard  errors  as  predicted  by  our
47:1584:108098:18:0:71:539:82:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:model atˆθ.  In order to compute the latter we simulated 10,000 draws fromF(α|ˆθ) and then

48:1601:108984:12:12:72:540:383:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:bid vectors for each type, simulating unobserved heterogeneityξ, and taking a weighted average according
48:1602:109088:12:45:72:404:371:10:g_d0_f7:10:g_d0_f7:F:to the probability that each bid is selected into the sample of observed bids.
48:1603:109166:45:24:72:482:326:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:weighted their bids according to the probability of being observed in each state.
48:1604:109247:24:18:72:540:302:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:The results in Table 6 suggests that our results fit the data reasonably well, though there
48:1605:109338:18:18:72:540:284:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:is some divergence, in particular for the higher–end cameras in the market.  We believe this
48:1606:109430:18:18:72:540:266:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:to be largely a function of the parametric compromises we made in order to focus on the
48:1607:109517:18:18:72:540:248:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:sharply identified set of 264 bidders who bid on multiple different resolution types.  However
48:1608:109611:18:18:72:540:230:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:for 6MP to 8MP cameras, which make up the bulk of our sample, we match these moments
48:1609:109695:18:18:72:540:212:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:quite closely.  Note that the moments are out-of-sample in that they incorporate bidders who
48:1610:109787:18:51:72:449:194:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:are observed once but then exit; these bidders are not used in estimation.
48:1611:109861:51:36:72:194:143:17:g_d0_f2:17:g_d0_f2:C:6    Conclusion
48:1612:109876:36:18:72:539:107:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:This  paper  offers  a  flexible  demand  system  for  the  study  of  auction  marketsas  markets.
48:1613:109975:18:18:72:540:89:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We developed a notion of equilibrium in such markets and proved its existence, and in turn
48:1614:110065:18:0:72:540:71:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:were  able  to  characterize  the  conditions  under  which  bidders’  actions  can  be  inverted  to
49:1615:110168:0:18:72:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:infer  their  private  type.   While  this  is  sufficient  for  identification  if  we  treat  auctions  as
49:1616:110276:18:18:72:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:independent,  isolated  draws  from  a  distribution,  in  an  auction  marketplace  we  also  need
49:1617:110375:18:18:72:540:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:to account for the selection of bidders into the observed and identified set.  Subject to the
49:1618:110468:18:19:72:540:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:constraints of non-participation, we are able to partially identify the distribution of types by
49:1619:110564:19:18:72:540:598:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:explicitly modeling this selection as a function of observable equilibrium objects.  We show
49:1620:110656:18:18:72:540:580:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:that this result extends to accommodate familiar features of auction data and demand models
49:1621:110747:18:18:72:540:562:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:in fixed-price markets,  including data limitations,  random coefficient demand,  unobserved
49:1622:110839:18:23:72:283:544:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:heterogeneity, and latent outside options.
49:1623:110881:23:19:72:540:521:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:The selection correction turns out to be an important source of flexibility in the model.  It
49:1624:110974:19:18:72:540:502:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:allows us to accommodate standard limitations of auction data.  It also gives the econome-
49:1625:111064:18:18:72:540:484:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:trician flexibility to pick and choose sources of variation in the data — in this case particular
49:1626:111161:18:23:72:302:466:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:histories — that they trust for identification.
49:1627:111208:23:18:72:540:443:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:A second important source of flexibility in the model is that we have made all the substitution
49:1628:111303:18:18:72:539:425:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:between products occurinter-temporally.  High-dimensional preferences are thus projected
49:1629:111391:18:19:72:540:407:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:down  to  a  valuation  for  the  current  product  and  a  continuation  value  which  ,  thanks  to
49:1630:111492:19:18:72:540:388:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:the Markov dynamics of the game, we can model in a straightforward way.  These Markov
49:1631:111577:18:18:72:540:370:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:dynamics also give us the flexibility to extend the state space of the game to incorporate
49:1632:111667:18:23:72:539:352:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:arbitrarypublicsignals about the state of the market on which bidder behavior may depend.
49:1633:111756:23:18:72:540:329:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We illustrated much of this flexibility in an application to the auction market for compact
49:1634:111847:18:18:72:540:311:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:cameras on eBay.  There we estimated the distribution of types for a utility function that
49:1635:111937:18:19:72:540:293:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:looked a lot like the kind you might estimate in a fixed-price market using standard methods
49:1636:112029:19:18:72:540:274:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:in industrial organization. While we were able to document a substantial bias in the estimates
49:1637:112123:18:18:72:540:256:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of consumer surplus that would come out of an alternative, static model, as well as match
49:1638:112212:18:18:72:540:238:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:out-of sample moments of the bid distribution, the main objective was to illustrate the kinds
49:1639:112305:18:18:72:540:220:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of judgment calls faced by an econometrician applying our method, which can accommodate
49:1640:112392:18:18:72:540:202:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:a wide array of data limitations, utility functions, information structures, and assumptions
49:1641:112484:18:24:72:186:184:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:about outside options.
49:1642:112506:24:18:72:540:160:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Our contribution — the development of a demand system for auction markets — is meant
49:1643:112590:18:18:72:540:142:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:to mirror similar work in fixed-price markets, and to a similar end:  the structural estimation
49:1644:112685:18:18:72:540:124:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of demand allows us to do counterfactuals of both private and public interest.  Though we
49:1645:112774:18:18:72:540:106:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:have developed a flexible framework, there remain several open directions for future work:
49:1646:112864:18:0:72:540:88:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:we believe that our framework would generalize naturally to multi-unit demand, in which
50:1647:112953:0:18:72:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:bidders may shade against the opportunity cost of moving further down their marginal utility
50:1648:113045:18:18:72:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:curve.  This is an important direction for the modeling of ad auctions and treasury auctions.
50:1649:113138:18:18:72:540:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:There are also unmet challenges in the modeling of substitution across auctions within-period
50:1650:113231:18:19:72:540:617:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:rather than inter-temporally.  Auction markets are a pervasive mechanism for the allocation
50:1651:113322:19:18:72:540:598:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of goods and services, and beyond our contribution there remains much work to be done to
50:1652:113410:18:51:72:398:580:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:understand competition between and substitution among them.

63:2246:137739:51:40:72:235:366:17:g_d0_f2:17:g_d0_f2:C:B    Data Appendix
63:2247:137757:40:32:72:199:326:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:B.1    Data Source
63:2248:137775:32:18:72:540:294:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We used data from eBay auctions for compact cameras that was purchased from Terapeak,
63:2249:137860:18:18:72:540:276:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:a private company that uses eBay data to offer analytics tools for sellers on the platform.
63:2250:137951:18:18:72:540:258:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:Our data included listing, seller, and bidder attributes as documented in Table 1 from the
63:2251:138041:18:45:72:125:240:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:main text.
63:2252:138051:45:31:72:260:195:14:g_d0_f2:14:g_d0_f2:C:B.2    Sample Construction
63:2253:138077:31:18:72:540:164:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:We restricted attention to auctions fornewcompact cameras that ended between the dates
63:2254:138163:18:37:71:539:146:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:B:of Feb 5 and May 6, 2007.  By way of data cleaning we also imposed the following restrictions:
63:2255:138257:37:18:86:540:109:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:1.  We were somewhat concerned that we may have been observing some “shill” bidding
63:2256:138340:18:18:101:540:91:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:by sellers intent on raising revenues.  We used the following rather coarse procedure to
63:2257:138428:18:0:101:540:73:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:detect such bidding behavior:  for any given bidder, if they won at least five auctions
64:2258:138517:0:18:101:540:671:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:and at 80% of them were from the same seller, then we flagged them as a shill bidder.
64:2259:138602:18:18:101:540:653:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:We excluded all auctions in which a so-designated shill bidder was among the set of
64:2260:138685:18:28:101:190:635:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:observed bidders.
64:2261:138702:28:19:86:540:607:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:2.  There are many senses in which a bid may be an “outlier”.  We excluded all winning
64:2262:138788:19:18:101:540:588:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:bids that were more than twice the sale price of the listing (either the second-highest
64:2263:138875:18:28:101:336:570:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:bid or the reserve price, whichever is greater).
64:2264:138923:28:18:86:540:542:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:3.  Though  we  did  not  exclude  auctions  that  used  the  Auction-Buy-it-Now  feature,  we
64:2265:139017:18:18:101:540:524:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:did exclude auctions that ended with the execution of the BIN option.  This option
64:2266:139099:18:18:101:540:506:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:disappears  once  the  first  bid  is  made,  so  those  listings  function  as  regular  auctions
64:2267:139197:18:18:101:540:488:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:afterwards.  See Ackerberg et al. (2009) for a fuller treatment of Auction-Buy-it-Now
64:2268:139282:18:28:101:147:470:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:auctions.
64:2269:139291:28:18:86:540:442:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:4.  We drop listings for which we are missing data on attributes (e.g., zoom, resolution),
64:2270:139381:18:18:101:540:424:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:for  which  those  attributes  are  unreasonable  or  technically  impossible,  or  where  the
64:2271:139475:18:0:101:250:406:12:g_d0_f3:12:g_d0_f3:A:product line is not indicated.
